<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你遗失了你的一段永恒，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>踏入这里，朋友啊，这里，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这里一切尚不<u>存在</u>；你心思分散，</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>第一次在万有中，心思分散、心不在焉，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>种种无尽的天性的彰显，你抓不住，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>就像抓不住这里的任何一件东西一样；</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>从已经接纳你的那个循环里，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>有一种不安，以喑哑的重力</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>将你向下拖出，在被计数的时间里——：</span><u><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这些，每每在夜里将我惊醒，像入室的窃贼</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn3'
href="#_ftn3" name="_ftnref3" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[③]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我可以这么说吗？你归来，只是</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>出于纡尊降贵，出于慷慨，出于充盈，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>因为你这般自信，这般存身于自己的内心，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>你四处走动，像个孩子，并不害怕</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>那些人们为他做下什么的地方——：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>哦不：你在请求。这些就这般</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";

mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>一个责备，你作为亡灵所背负的，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>我的最后最可怜的心室，——</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>一直进入你的凝望；巨大地停留在镜前，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>不说“是我”，而说“这是”。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>最后，你的凝望就这样毫无好奇，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>就这样一无所有，就这样真正的贫穷，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>于是你的凝望不再渴望你本人：圣洁地。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>我想要这样留住你，就像你</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>将自己置入镜中，深深地进入，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>远离一切</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn5' href="#_ftn5"
name="_ftnref5" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑤]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>。为什么你又别样地到来？</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>为什么你要收回自己？为什么你想</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>说服我，让我相信你颈上的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>琥珀项链里，<span style='color:black'>依然有某种重来自</span></span><span
lang=DE style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>那些重，仿佛那些重从未在对面</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>归于宁静的画像里存在过？</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>为什么</span><span lang=DE style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你用你的身姿向我展现一个恶兆？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>是什么令你将你肉体的轮廓</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>像一只手的掌纹一样铺陈，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>以至于除了命运我再也看不见它？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>来到这烛光下吧！我并不害怕</span><span lang=DE

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你：你内心的感觉也甜甜的。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我要在他身上控诉一切人：男人。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>如果我心深处某个地方升起一个</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>曾经的孩童的形象，我并不认识的、</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>或许是我童年里最纯洁的孩童：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我也不想去详究。我只想</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>看也不看就用它塑造成一个天使，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我只想将这个天使抛入提醒上帝的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那些呼号天使</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn8' href="#_ftn8"
name="_ftnref8" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑧]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>的第一列。</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>痛苦已经持续得太长太久，</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>无人能够忍受；让我们感到过于沉重的，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>自称是正义，却滋生于非正义。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>守住船头的尼刻女神</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn9'

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>有可能发生的是，他不再将血液高举，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>血液因自身的沉重而失去价值</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>因为一个古老的敌意在某处</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>存在于生活和伟大的劳动之间。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我愿看清并说出这个敌意：帮助我。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>不要回来。如果你能够忍受，你就</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>死在死者之中吧。死者是忙碌的。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>但请拨冗帮助我，愿你不会因此心思分散，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>就像最远之物偶尔帮助我那样：在我心中。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>原文参看：</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><a
href="http://www.zeno.org/Literatur/M/Rilke,+Rainer+Maria/Gedichte/Requiem/F%C3%BCr+eine+Freundin">http://www.zeno.org/Literatur/M/Rilke,+Rainer+Maria/Gedichte/Requiem/F%C3%BCr+eine+Freundin</a><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 align=left style='text-align:left'><span style='font-family:黑体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Arial Black"'>祭沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德伯爵</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:
ftn10' href="#_ftn10" name="_ftnref10" title=""><span
class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=DE><span style='mso-special-character:
footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑩]<![endif]></span></span></span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>真的我从未见过你？我的心感到</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这般沉重</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn11' href="#_ftn11"
name="_ftnref11" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[11]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>，因你，如同因被推迟的</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>太过沉重的开始。我愿开始将你</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>讲述，如今已是死者的你；你啊，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>欢欣而激情的死者。这一切真如</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你料想的那样轻松，抑或</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>不再去生依然远离死去？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你以为，在那里你会更好地占有，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>因为那里无人在意占有。你觉得，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那里你会置身于对面风景的内部，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这里那风景却像一幅画总在你面前闭合，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那里你会从内部出来走入你的所爱，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>然后离去，穿过一切，强健而摇曳。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>啊，愿你如今向你稚气的错误里</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>凭添假象，还并不太久。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>愿你，放松在忧伤的潮流，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>沉迷地、半梦半醒地，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>在围绕远方众星的运行中</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>寻得欢乐，你从这里搬移到</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你梦寐的死去里的欢乐。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>在这里是多么近啊，好友，你与那欢乐。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>在这里是多么安居啊，那个，你意料中的，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>你强烈的渴望中真诚的</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>欢乐。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那时你，满怀对幸与不幸的失望，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>钻入自己的里面，然后带着一种见识</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>疲惫地升上来，在你幽暗的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>发现物的重量下摇摇欲碎：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你背负着它，它，你不曾认清的，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你背负着欢乐，背负着你的小小救主</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>施与重担，穿越你的血液，渡到对岸。</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn12'
href="#_ftn12" name="_ftnref12" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[12]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd;text-indent:10.5pt;mso-char-indent-count:
1.0;mso-char-indent-size:10.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>为什么你没有等待，等待那沉重</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>变得全然无法承负：那沉重骤变，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>因这般纯正而这般沉重？你可看见，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>或许瞬间之后就会临到你的事：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>当你猛然关上门，或许他</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>正在你的门前扶正他头上的冠冕？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='color:black;
mso-ansi-language:DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>这一声撞击，是怎样响彻了宇宙，</span><span
lang=DE style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>当某处一个敞开，被不耐所产生的</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>坚硬尖锐的气流砰然关闭。</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>谁能誓言，不在泥土中</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>一道裂痕也会穿过健康的种子？</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>谁曾探究，在驯服的动物心中</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>是否不是一种杀戮之欲淫邪闪现，</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>当这碰撞将一道电光投入它们的脑中？</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>谁识得这流动，从我们的行为</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>涌入对面的一个近端，</span><span lang=DE
style='color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:DE'>谁会与它同行，当一切都在先行？</span><span lang=DE

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这些属于你，你啊，艺术家；这三种</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>开敞的模式。看呐，这是第一种的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>铸件：你情感四周的空间；那是</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我从第二种里为你锻造出的直观，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>无所渴求的、伟大艺术家的直观；</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>而第三种，第一股颤动的钟铜</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>从心的白热里出来，刚刚涌入</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>其中，你就亲手过早地将之</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>打碎——，那是一个死，被出色的劳动</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>深化，在其中铸成，那个自己的死，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>如此需要我们，因我们生活着死。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>除却这里没有哪里我们距它更近。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>这一切都是你的财富与友谊；</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你时常对此有预感；但后来</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这些模式的凹空却让你恐惧，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你伸手进去，空手而返，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>于是你开始抱怨。——啊诗人古老的诅咒，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那些应当说话的时候总是张口抱怨的诗人，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>他们的情感，他们总是论断，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>而不是培养；他们始终以为，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>凡是在他们心中成为悲或者喜的，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>他们都熟悉，都应该在诗歌里</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>报以惜或者赞。他们像病人一样，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>在感到疼痛的时候，使用那些</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>充满痛苦的语言去书写疼痛，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>而不是像大教堂的石匠顽强地</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>将自己转换成岩石的冷静一样，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>艰苦地将他们自己转化成词语。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>这就是拯救。只要你曾经看见</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>一</span></u><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>次，看见命运怎样进入诗行，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>一去不回，怎样在其中变成画像，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>仅仅是画像，仅仅是一个先祖，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你偶尔瞻仰时画框里的让你觉得</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>既像你又不像你的一个先祖——：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你也就会一直隐忍。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>思考那并不存在的</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>事，不过是小题大做，不过是一个</span><span lang=DE style='color:black;
mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>比喻式的责备的一个假象，<span style='color:black'>对你无所中伤</span>。</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>发生的事，就这样领先于</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我们的料想，因此我们从未追赶上它，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>从未获知它本真的形貌。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>不要羞惭，当坚持到终点的</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那些死者与你擦肩而过的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>时候，（终点意味着什么？）同他们</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>用眼色交谈吧，平静地，当作习俗，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>不要惧怕我们的悲哀会异样地成为</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你的负担，会使你在死者中显得醒目。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>伟大的词语，出自发生的事</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>依然可见的时代</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>，</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>并非为我们而存在。</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:4.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>谁还在言及胜利呢？忍耐就是一切。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 align=left style='text-align:left'><span style='font-family:黑体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Arial Black"'>安魂曲哀悼一个小男孩的死</span><a style='mso-footnote-id:
ftn15' href="#_ftn15" name="_ftnref15" title=""><span
class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=DE><span style='mso-special-character:
footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[15]<![endif]></span></span></span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我都牢记了些什么样的名字啊！</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>狗、母牛、大象，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>如今如此久如此远竟还能认出来，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>然后是斑马——，唉，何益？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>此刻驮着我，</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>如水位一样上升，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>超过了这一切。安宁了吗，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>已经知道，存在，无需</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>去向那理解中的幻境？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>而这已经开始的双手——</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

mso-ansi-language:DE'>你们偶尔会说：他答应……</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>就这样我强行与一切为伴。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>愿一切没有我却也心满意足，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>或者<span style='color:black'>把我挂在身上，</span>日渐哀伤。</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>如今我突然离开而去。</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>开始</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>一次新的学习，一个新的探问？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>或者此刻我该问</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>你们中的一切都怎样了？——此时我恐惧着。</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>房屋？我还从未这般正确理解过。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>房间？唉里面有这么多东西存在。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>……你啊母亲，究竟<u>谁</u>才是</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>狗？</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>甚至，我们在森林里找到浆果，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>此刻对我也是一个神奇的发现</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>那里一定会有死去的孩子，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>来和我一起游戏。那里总是有</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这些死去的孩子。先是躺在卧室里，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>像我一样躺着，变得不健康。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>健康……在这里听起来何等的好！可这还有意义吗？</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>在那里，我现在的地方，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我想，没有人患病。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>我患咽喉痛，已然这么久——</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>这里每一样都如一种新鲜的饮料。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>依然我没有看见那将我们啜饮的</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>……</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>被屏蔽，原文只好请参看：</span><span lang=DE
