<h2 align=left style='text-align:left'><span style='font-family:黑体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Arial Black"'>安魂曲</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><i><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>献给克拉拉·韦斯特霍夫</span></i><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn16'
href="#_ftn16" name="_ftnref16" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[16]<![endif]></span></span></span></a></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一个时刻起，尘世间有更多围绕着</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一个事物，围绕着一个花冠。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>片刻前这轻盈的叶……我在编结：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>而此刻这常春藤异常沉重，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>被晦暗充满，仿佛从</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我的事物中吸吮未来的黑夜。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>此刻我几乎因将临的黑夜而恐惧，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>孤独地伴着我制作的这个花冠，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>毫无预感，当藤蔓缠满</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>冠饰的时候，会有什么出现；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我完全只需要理解：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>有什么可能已经不在</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>。何等地迷失</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在从未觉察的念头里啊，里面那些神奇的事物，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>想必我已经见过一次……</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>……随流水飘走的，是孩子们在游戏中撕碎的鲜花；从张开的指缝掉落，一瓣又一瓣，一直落到花束再也无法辨认。一直落到余下的部分，被孩子们带回家，正好用来烧火。然后可能有一个人彻夜，在所有人都以为他已经沉睡的时候，为这破碎的鲜花垂泪。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>格蕾特尔，从最开初</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你就已经注定绝早地死，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>金发地死。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>久已注定，在你注定生之前。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因此主在你之前安排了一个姐姐，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>又安排了一个哥哥，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>藉此让你之前有两个亲近的人，那两个纯洁的人，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>他们昭示给你那个死，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>那个属于你的：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的死。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的姐姐哥哥被创造。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>只是，藉此让你习惯于死，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>让你借两个死亡时刻</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>与数千年来一直在恫吓你的</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>第三个死亡时刻和解。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>为你的死</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>生被重建；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>手，将花朵捆扎，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>目光，将玫瑰的红</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>与人的强大觉察，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它们被人塑造，被人重新销毁，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>被死两次<u>创造</u>，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>就在死径直向你本人，从</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>灯火渐熄的舞台走下之前。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>……它在可怕地走近你吗，亲爱的玩伴？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它可是你的敌人？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你可曾为它心头泪流？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它可曾将你从滚烫的枕</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>拖入闪烁的黑夜，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>拖入那个全家无人睡去的黑夜……？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它是什么模样？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你一定知道的。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你已经为它启程向故乡行去。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span>
<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你知道</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>扁桃开花的姿容，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你知道湖是蓝色的。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>许多事情，只有体验过初恋的女性</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>才能够感觉到，——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你都知道。大自然对你耳语，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在南方暮色苍茫的日子里，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>告诉你无尽的美，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一如从前，唯有那些有福的人</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>用有福的唇才能说出美，因为他们与美二者</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>拥有<u>一个</u>世界、<u>一个</u>声音——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>更轻轻地你已经觉察到这一切，——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>（啊，这无终的怒气是何等地</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>触碰着你无终的谦卑）。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的信来自南方，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因阳光而依然温暖，但孤苦伶仃，——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>最终你本人也跟随你疲惫</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>求助的信踏上行程；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因为你在光芒中并不开心，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>每种颜色落在你身上如同罪，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你生活在不耐之中，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因为你知道：这并非<u>全部</u>。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>生只是一个局部……属于何处？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>生只是一个色调……停于何处？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>生只是将意义关联到众多的</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>圆，属于向远处增长着的空间，——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>生只是一个梦的梦，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>梦醒却在别处。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>就这样你将生放手。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>巨大地你将生放手。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我们熟悉你的幼小。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>属于你的是如此稀少：一丝笑靥，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一根细小、总是略带忧郁、</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>温柔异常的头发，一个小小的房间——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>那个房间姐姐死去后让你感到空阔。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>其他的一切恍然只是你的衣裳，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>这就是此刻我的感觉，你啊安静的玩伴。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>然而<u>你曾经是</u></span><u><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>特别的多</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>。我们是偶尔知道的，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>当你傍晚出现在大厅里的时候；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我们偶尔知道：此刻想必有人在祷告；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一群人已经进入，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>一群跟随你的人，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因为你熟悉路途。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你想必已经熟悉路途，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你昨天就已经熟悉了……</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>最幼小的姊妹啊。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>看这里啊，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>这顶花冠是这般沉重。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>他们将会加戴给你</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>这顶沉重的花冠。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的棺椁能承受住它吗？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>假如你的棺椁</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因黑色的重量而断裂，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你衣裳的褶裥里</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>就会爬满</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>常春藤。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>远远地向上攀缘，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>围绕着你攀缘，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>汁液，在常春藤的藤蔓里涌动，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>用它的嘈杂撩动你；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你是如此童贞。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>但你已经不再闭合。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你已经被拉长已经松弛。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你肉体的门扇扇虚掩，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>于是湿漉漉地</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>常春藤抬脚踏入……</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span>
<span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>—</span> <span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>—</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>仿佛一队队</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>修女，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>彼此引导</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>藉着黑色的绳索，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因为你的身内一片晦暗，你啊泉井。</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的血液空荡荡的</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>通道里，</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>常春藤<u>拥挤向你的心；</u></span><u><span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>旧日你温柔的痛苦</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>带着苍白的喜悦与回忆</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>彼此相遇的地方</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>，——</span><u><span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它们漫游着，仿佛在祈祷，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在进入你的心，那颗心，寂然无声，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>晦暗地，向一切敞开。</span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>但这顶花冠却让我感到沉重，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在光亮中，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在活人中，在这里我身旁；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它的重量</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>将不复存在，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在我将它放在你身上的时候。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>大地充满了平衡</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>，</span><u><span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的大地</span></u><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>这顶花冠沉重，因眷恋它的我的眼，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>沉重，因我为它</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>所进行的工作；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>所有看见它的人所心生的惧怕，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>都黏附在它上面。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>将它拿给你吧，因为它一被做成，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它就属于你。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>将它拿离我吧。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>让我孤独！它恰如一个过客……</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>几乎让我感到羞愧。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你也感到害怕吗，格蕾特尔？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你不再能够走路了？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你不再能够站在这陋室里我的身边？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的脚疼吗？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>就这样停留在此刻一切全在一起的地方吧，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>明天有人会将花冠给你带去，宝贝，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>穿过枝叶凋零的林荫路。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>有人会将花冠给你带去，安心等待吧，——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>明天有人还会给你带去更多东西。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>即使明天风狂雨骤，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>也不会对花有太多伤害。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>有人会将花给你带去。你有权利</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>安全拥有它们，宝贝，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>即使明天它们会变成黑色会残败不堪</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>会永久消逝。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>不要因此而担忧。你将不会再</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>辨别出什么在上升什么在下沉；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>颜料已干，色调已空，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>甚至你也根本就不会知道，是谁</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>给你带去所有这些花。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>此刻你已经熟悉<u>那个他者</u>，每当我们</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在黑暗中将它抓住，他就会驱逐我们；</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>从那个你所<u>渴望</u>的，你被救赎</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>成某个你所<u>拥有</u>的。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我们之中你曾经形象幼小，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>或许此刻你已是一片成熟的森林，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>林叶间有风有声音。——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>相信我，玩伴，暴力不会再临到你：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>你的死已经衰老，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>在你的生开始时；</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>因此死紧抓住生，</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><u><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>以便生生不过死。</span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>……………………</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>有什么在我周围飘荡吗？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>是夜风走了进来？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我没有颤抖。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我坚强而孤独。——</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我今天创作了什么？</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>……常春藤叶，我在黄昏时取来，编结着，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>弯折着，最终使它完全驯服。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>它依然闪动着黑色的光。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我的力量</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:6.0gd'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>盘旋在花冠里。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>原文请参看：</span><span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></p>

lang=EN-US>4</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>日</span><span lang=EN-US>17</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>时</span><span lang=EN-US>53</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>分</span><span
lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>秒</span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn2>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn2' href="#_ftnref2"
name="_ftn2" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[②]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>德国女画家褒拉</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>·</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>莫德松</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>–</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>贝克尔</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>（</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'>Paula Modersohn-Becker</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>1876.2.8 – 1907.11.20</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>）</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US>1900</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>年，褒拉和好友女雕塑家克拉拉·韦斯特霍夫（</span><span
lang=EN-US>Clara Westhoff</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>）结识了在沃尔普斯维德（</span><span
lang=EN-US>Worpswede</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>）借住画家奥托·莫德松（</span><span
lang=EN-US>Otto Modersohn</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>）家中的诗人里尔克。次年，褒拉嫁给奥托·莫德松，而后，里尔克娶克拉拉·韦斯特霍夫为妻。</span><span
lang=EN-US>1906</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>年，褒拉画出若干当时被视为“空前的”女画家裸体自画像。同年，褒拉也为里尔克画出一幅肖像画。</span><span
lang=EN-US>1907</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>年</span><span lang=EN-US>11</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>月</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>日，褒拉生下一女，</span><span
lang=EN-US>20</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>日，死于血栓。时隔将近一年，</span><span lang=EN-US>1908</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>年</span><span lang=EN-US>10</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>月</span><span
lang=EN-US>31</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>日起，里尔克用三天时间，写下这首《安魂曲》。这是一首五音步抑扬格的无韵长诗。</span><span
lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn7>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn8>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn8' href="#_ftnref8"
name="_ftn8" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑧]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>《旧约·以赛亚书》第</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>6</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>章</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>2–3</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>节：“其上有撒拉弗侍立。各有六个翅膀。用两个翅膀遮脸，两个翅膀遮脚，两个翅膀飞翔。彼此呼喊说，圣哉，圣哉，圣哉，万军之耶和华。他的荣光充满全地。”</span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>撒拉弗，即基督教九级天使中阶位最高的大天使。</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn9>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn9' href="#_ftnref9"
name="_ftn9" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑨]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>尼刻：</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>Nike</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>，古希腊语为</span><span lang=DE
style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>Ν&#943;κη</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>，古希腊胜利女神的名字（此名词也是一种运动鞋的商标，被汉译成“耐克”）。诗中此处指称装饰在船头的胜利女神像。</span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn10>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn10' href="#_ftnref10"
name="_ftn10" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[⑩]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德伯爵（</span><span
lang=EN-US>1887. 6. 9 – 1906. 10. 9</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>），诗人、翻译家，画家利奥波德·卡尔克罗伊德之子，翻译过波德莱尔的《恶之花》等。</span><span
lang=EN-US>1906</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>年因不堪兵役之苦而自杀。里尔克与沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德并不相识，只是听闻事件之后有感而发。后托请他的岛屿出版社编辑安东·基彭贝格（</span><span
lang=EN-US>Anton Kippenberg</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US>1874–1950</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>）将此诗手抄件转赠给沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德的母亲。从里尔克此诗的行文来看，无疑，里尔克读过沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德的诗集。</span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn11>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn11' href="#_ftnref11"
name="_ftn11" title=""><span class=MsoFootnoteReference><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-special-character:footnote'><![if !supportFootnotes]>[11]<![endif]></span></span></span></a><span
lang=EN-US> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>此诗中的“沉重”，亦含“艰难”意。请读者酌情替换。</span></p>

</div>

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn12>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn12' href="#_ftnref12"

<div style='mso-element:footnote' id=ftn16>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><a style='mso-footnote-id:ftn16' href="#_ftnref16"

lang=EN-US style='mso-ansi-language:DE'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;

"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>·</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>韦斯特霍夫</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>（</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

DE'>）</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>即里尔克日后的发妻。格蕾特尔</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>·</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>柯特迈尔</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>（</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:

"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>），</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>克拉拉的朋友</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:DE'>，</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>1900</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:DE'>年亡故，</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>事迹不详。里尔克在</span><span
lang=EN-US>1900</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>年</span><span lang=EN-US>11</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>月</span><span lang=EN-US>20</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>日的日记中写道：</span></p>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><span lang=EN-US><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>克拉拉·</span><span
lang=EN-US>W</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>今天写信提到一个黑色的常春藤花冠，她所讲述的重新成为一首完整的诗。她是怎样谈及那黑色的花冠的啊，那花冠，是她毫无预感地从她房屋的山墙灰色的十一月的风里取来，此刻在这斗室里变得非凡的庄重，一个自为之物，一个骤然之物，一个显得渐渐沉重之物，仿佛正在尽饮一切哀伤，这房间空气里的、这晨光胧明里的哀伤。而这一切都应当陈放在可怜少女的薄薄的木棺上，那在南方、在阳光的手中死去的少女。黑色的花冠或许会压碎棺椁，花冠长长的藤蔓或许会攀上白色的殓衣，与合十的手生在一起，与心生在一起，那颗心，充满凝固的血液，也变得黑色、平坦，在死者的晨光胧明里与常春藤叶的心几乎无法区分……在血液空荡荡的通道，常春藤将穿行着，叶片叠着叶片，在长长的藤蔓上，如一群修女，在一根绳索上互相倚靠。</span></p>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText style='text-indent:18.0pt'><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>我愿用这幅画面写一首安魂曲。</span></p>

<p class=MsoFootnoteText><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:
DE'>（</span><span lang=DE style='mso-ansi-language:DE'>Rainer Maria Rilke, <i>Tagebücher
aus der Frühzeit</i>. hrsg. von Ruth Sieber-Rilke und Carl Sieber. Leipzig,
Insel-Verlag, 1942. </span><span lang=EN-US>S. 388f</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-hansi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>）。</span></p>
